## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Execute-ProcessAsUser.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser"
title: "Execute-ProcessAsUser · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Execute a process with a logged in user account, by using a scheduled task, to provide interaction with user in the SYSTEM context.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Execute-ProcessAsUser [[-UserName] <String>] [-Path] <String> [[-TempPath] <String>] [[-Parameters] <String>]
 [-SecureParameters] [[-RunLevel] <String>] [-Wait] [-PassThru] [[-WorkingDirectory] <String>]
 [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Execute a process with a logged in user account, by using a scheduled task, to provide interaction with user in the SYSTEM context.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Execute-ProcessAsUser -UserName 'CONTOSO\User' -Path "$PSHOME\powershell.exe" -Parameters "-Command `"& { & 'C:\Test\Script.ps1'; Exit `$LastExitCode }`"" -Wait

```

Execute process under a user account by specifying a username under which to execute it.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Execute-ProcessAsUser -Path "$PSHOME\powershell.exe" -Parameters "-Command `"& { & 'C:\Test\Script.ps1'; Exit `$LastExitCode }`"" -Wait

```

Execute process under a user account by using the default active logged in user that was detected when the toolkit was launched.

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Execute-ProcessAsUser -Path "$PSHOME\powershell.exe" -Parameters "-Command `"& { & 'C:\Test\Script.ps1'; Exit `$LastExitCode }`"" -RunLevel 'LeastPrivilege'

```

Execute process using 'LeastPrivilege' under a user account by using the default active logged in user that was detected when the toolkit was launched.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -UserName [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-username "Direct link to -UserName")

Logged in Username under which to run the process from.
Default is: The active console user.
If no console user exists but users are logged in, such as on terminal servers, then the first logged-in non-console user.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: $RunAsActiveUser.NTAccount
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Path [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-path "Direct link to -Path")

Path to the file being executed.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 2
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -TempPath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-temppath "Direct link to -TempPath")

Path to the temporary directory used to store the script to be executed as user.
If using a user writable directory, ensure you select -RunLevel 'LeastPrivilege'.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 3
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Parameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-parameters "Direct link to -Parameters")

Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -SecureParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-secureparameters "Direct link to -SecureParameters")

Hides all parameters passed to the executable from the Toolkit log file.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -RunLevel [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-runlevel "Direct link to -RunLevel")

Specifies the level of user rights that Task Scheduler uses to run the task.
The acceptable values for this parameter are:

- HighestAvailable: Tasks run by using the highest available privileges (Admin privileges for Administrators).
Default Value.

- LeastPrivilege: Tasks run by using the least-privileged user account (LUA) privileges.


```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 5
Default value: HighestAvailable
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Wait [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-wait "Direct link to -Wait")

Wait for the process, launched by the scheduled task, to complete execution before accepting more input.
Default is $false.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -PassThru [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-passthru "Direct link to -PassThru")

```

### -WorkingDirectory [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-workingdirectory "Direct link to -WorkingDirectory")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

Required: False
Position: 6

Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Execute-ProcessAsUser\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

Continue if an error is encountered.
Default is $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Exit-Script.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script"
title: "Exit-Script · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Exit the script, perform cleanup actions, and pass an exit code to the parent process.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Exit-Script [[-ExitCode] <Int32>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Always use when exiting the script to ensure cleanup actions are performed.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Exit-Script

```

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Exit-Script -ExitCode 1618

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -ExitCode [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#-exitcode "Direct link to -ExitCode")

The exit code to be passed from the script to the parent process, e.g.
SCCM

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Int32
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: 0
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Exit-Script\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-IniValue.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue"
title: "Get-IniValue · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Parses an INI file and returns the value of the specified section and key.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-IniValue [-FilePath] <String> [-Section] <String> [-Key] <String> [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Parses an INI file and returns the value of the specified section and key.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-IniValue\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-IniValue -FilePath "$envProgramFilesX86\IBM\Notes\notes.ini" -Section 'Notes' -Key 'KeyFileName'

```

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-InstalledApplication.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication"
title: "Get-InstalledApplication · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Retrieves information about installed applications.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-InstalledApplication [[-Name] <String[]>] [-Exact] [-WildCard] [-RegEx] [[-ProductCode] <String>]
 [-IncludeUpdatesAndHotfixes] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Retrieves information about installed applications by querying the registry.
You can specify an application name, a product code, or both.

Returns information about application publisher, name & version, product code, uninstall string, install source, location, date, and application architecture.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-InstalledApplication -Name 'Adobe Flash'

```

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-InstalledApplication -ProductCode '{1AD147D0-BE0E-3D6C-AC11-64F6DC4163F1}'

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -Name [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-InstalledApplication\#-name "Direct link to -Name")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-LoggedOnUser.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser"
title: "Get-LoggedOnUser · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Get session details for all local and RDP logged on users.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-LoggedOnUser [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Get session details for all local and RDP logged on users using Win32 APIs.
Get the following session details:
NTAccount, SID, UserName, DomainName, SessionId, SessionName, ConnectState, IsCurrentSession, IsConsoleSession, IsUserSession, IsActiveUserSession
IsRdpSession, IsLocalAdmin, LogonTime, IdleTime, DisconnectTime, ClientName, ClientProtocolType, ClientDirectory, ClientBuildNumber

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-LoggedOnUser

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

### None [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#none "Direct link to None")

### You cannot pipe objects to this function. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#you-cannot-pipe-objects-to-this-function "Direct link to You cannot pipe objects to this function.")

## OUTPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#outputs "Direct link to OUTPUTS")

### None [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#none-1 "Direct link to None")

### This function does not return any objects. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#this-function-does-not-return-any-objects "Direct link to This function does not return any objects.")

## NOTES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#notes "Direct link to NOTES")

Description of ConnectState property:

Value Description

* * *

Active A user is logged on to the session.
ConnectQuery The session is in the process of connecting to a client.
Connected A client is connected to the session.
Disconnected The session is active, but the client has disconnected from it.
Down The session is down due to an error.
Idle The session is waiting for a client to connect.
Initializing The session is initializing.
Listening The session is listening for connections.
Reset The session is being reset.
Shadowing This session is shadowing another session.

Description of IsActiveUserSession property:

- If a console user exists, then that will be the active user session.
- If no console user exists but users are logged in, such as on terminal servers, then the first logged-in non-console user that has ConnectState either 'Active' or 'Connected' is the active user.

Description of IsRdpSession property:

- Gets a value indicating whether the user is associated with an RDP client session.

Description of IsLocalAdmin property:

- Checks whether the user is a member of the Administrators group

## RELATED LINKS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser\#related-links "Direct link to RELATED LINKS")

[https://psappdeploytoolkit.com](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/)

- [DESCRIPTION](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-LoggedOnUser#description)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiExitCodeMessage\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiExitCodeMessage\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiExitCodeMessage\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-MsiTableProperty.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty"
title: "Get-MsiTableProperty · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Get all of the properties from a Windows Installer database table or the Summary Information stream and return as a custom object.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

### TableInfo (Default) [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#tableinfo-default "Direct link to TableInfo (Default)")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-MsiTableProperty -Path <String> [-TransformPath <String[]>] [-Table <String>]
 [-TablePropertyNameColumnNum <Int32>] [-TablePropertyValueColumnNum <Int32>] [-ContinueOnError <Boolean>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

### SummaryInfo [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#summaryinfo "Direct link to SummaryInfo")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-MsiTableProperty -Path <String> [-TransformPath <String[]>] [-GetSummaryInformation]
 [-ContinueOnError <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Use the Windows Installer object to read all of the properties from a Windows Installer database table or the Summary Information stream.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-MsiTableProperty -Path 'C:\Package\AppDeploy.msi' -TransformPath 'C:\Package\AppDeploy.mst'

```

Retrieve all of the properties from the default 'Property' table.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-MsiTableProperty -Path 'C:\Package\AppDeploy.msi' -TransformPath 'C:\Package\AppDeploy.mst' -Table 'Property' | Select-Object -ExpandProperty ProductCode

```

Retrieve all of the properties from the 'Property' table and then pipe to Select-Object to select the ProductCode property.

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-MsiTableProperty -Path 'C:\Package\AppDeploy.msi' -GetSummaryInformation

```

Retrieves the Summary Information for the Windows Installer database.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -Path [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-path "Direct link to -Path")

The fully qualified path to an database file.
Supports .msi and .msp files.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: Named
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -TransformPath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-transformpath "Direct link to -TransformPath")

The fully qualified path to a list of MST file(s) which should be applied to the MSI file.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String[]
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Table [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-table "Direct link to -Table")

The name of the the MSI table from which all of the properties must be retrieved.
Default is: 'Property'.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: TableInfo
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
        Default value: $(If ([IO.Path]::GetExtension($Path) -eq '.msi') {
                'Property'
            }
            Else {
                'MsiPatchMetadata'
            })
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -TablePropertyNameColumnNum [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-tablepropertynamecolumnnum "Direct link to -TablePropertyNameColumnNum")

Default is: 1 for MSIs and 2 for MSPs.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Int32
Parameter Sets: TableInfo
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
        Default value: $(If ([IO.Path]::GetExtension($Path) -eq '.msi') {
                1
            }
            Else {
                2
            })
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -TablePropertyValueColumnNum [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-tablepropertyvaluecolumnnum "Direct link to -TablePropertyValueColumnNum")

            }

                3
            })

Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -GetSummaryInformation [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-MsiTableProperty\#-getsummaryinformation "Direct link to -GetSummaryInformation")

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture"
title: "Get-PEFileArchitecture · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Determine if a PE file is a 32-bit or a 64-bit file.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-PEFileArchitecture [-FilePath] <FileInfo[]> [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [-PassThru] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Determine if a PE file is a 32-bit or a 64-bit file by examining the file's image file header.

PE file extensions: .exe, .dll, .ocx, .drv, .sys, .scr, .efi, .cpl, .fon

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-PEFileArchitecture -FilePath "$env:windir\notepad.exe"

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -FilePath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PEFileArchitecture\#-filepath "Direct link to -FilePath")

Path to the PE file to examine.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: FileInfo[]
Parameter Sets: (All)

Position: 1

Accept wildcard characters: False

```

Parameter Sets: (All)

Required: False

Accept wildcard characters: False

```

Get the file object, attach a property indicating the file binary type, and write to pipeline

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-PendingReboot.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot"
title: "Get-PendingReboot · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Get the pending reboot status on a local computer.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-PendingReboot [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Check WMI and the registry to determine if the system has a pending reboot operation from any of the following:
a) Component Based Servicing (Vista, Windows 2008)
b) Windows Update / Auto Update (XP, Windows 2003 / 2008)
c) SCCM 2012 Clients (DetermineIfRebootPending WMI method)
d) App-V Pending Tasks (global based Appv 5.0 SP2)
e) Pending File Rename Operations (XP, Windows 2003 / 2008)

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-PendingReboot

```

Returns custom object with following properties:

- ComputerName
- LastBootUpTime
- IsSystemRebootPending
- IsCBServicingRebootPending
- IsWindowsUpdateRebootPending
- IsSCCMClientRebootPending
- IsFileRenameRebootPending
- PendingFileRenameOperations
- ErrorMsg

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
(Get-PendingReboot).IsSystemRebootPending

```

Returns boolean value determining whether or not there is a pending reboot operation.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-PendingReboot\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-RegistryKey.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey"
title: "Get-RegistryKey · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Retrieves value names and value data for a specified registry key or optionally, a specific value.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey [-Key] <String> [[-Value] <String>] [-Wow6432Node] [[-SID] <String>] [-ReturnEmptyKeyIfExists]
 [-DoNotExpandEnvironmentNames] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Retrieves value names and value data for a specified registry key or optionally, a specific value.

If the registry key does not exist or contain any values, the function will return $null by default.
To test for existence of a registry key path, use built-in Test-Path cmdlet.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey -Key 'HKLM:SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Uninstall\{1AD147D0-BE0E-3D6C-AC11-64F6DC4163F1}'

```

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey -Key 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows NT\CurrentVersion\Image File Execution Options\iexplore.exe'

```

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey -Key 'HKLM:Software\Wow6432Node\Microsoft\Microsoft SQL Server Compact Edition\v3.5' -Value 'Version'

```

### EXAMPLE 4 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#example-4 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 4")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey -Key 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Session Manager\Environment' -Value 'Path' -DoNotExpandEnvironmentNames

```

Returns %ProgramFiles%\\Java instead of C:\\Program Files\\Java

### EXAMPLE 5 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#example-5 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 5")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-RegistryKey -Key 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Example' -Value '(Default)'

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -Key [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#-key "Direct link to -Key")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

Specify this switch to read the 32-bit registry (Wow6432Node) on 64-bit systems.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -SID [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#-sid "Direct link to -SID")

The security identifier (SID) for a user.
Specifying this parameter will convert a HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER registry key to the HKEY\_USERS$SID format.

Specify this parameter from the Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers function to read/edit HKCU registry settings for all users on the system.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 3
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ReturnEmptyKeyIfExists [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#-returnemptykeyifexists "Direct link to -ReturnEmptyKeyIfExists")

Return the registry key if it exists but it has no property/value pairs underneath it.
Default is: $false.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -DoNotExpandEnvironmentNames [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RegistryKey\#-donotexpandenvironmentnames "Direct link to -DoNotExpandEnvironmentNames")

Return unexpanded REG\_EXPAND\_SZ values.
Default is: $false.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: SwitchParameter
Parameter Sets: (All)

Required: False
Position: Named
Default value: False

Accept wildcard characters: False

```

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RunningProcesses\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Gets the processes that are running from a custom list of process objects and also adds a property called ProcessDescription.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RunningProcesses\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RunningProcesses\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Gets the processes that are running from a custom list of process objects and also adds a property called ProcessDescription.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-RunningProcesses\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-SchedulerTask.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask"
title: "Get-SchedulerTask · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Retrieve all details for scheduled tasks on the local computer.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-SchedulerTask [[-TaskName] <String>] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Retrieve all details for scheduled tasks on the local computer using schtasks.exe.
All property names have spaces and colons removed.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-SchedulerTask

```

To display a list of all scheduled task properties.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-SchedulerTask | Out-GridView

```

To display a grid view of all scheduled task properties.

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-SchedulerTask | Select-Object -Property TaskName

```

To display a list of all scheduled task names.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -TaskName [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#-taskname "Direct link to -TaskName")

Specify the name of the scheduled task to retrieve details for.
Uses regex match to find scheduled task.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

Continue if an error is encountered.
Default: $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Boolean
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: True
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

### None [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#none "Direct link to None")

### You cannot pipe objects to this function. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#you-cannot-pipe-objects-to-this-function "Direct link to You cannot pipe objects to this function.")

## OUTPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#outputs "Direct link to OUTPUTS")

### PSOjbect. This function returns a PSObject with all scheduled task properties. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#psojbect-this-function-returns-a-psobject-with-all-scheduled-task-properties "Direct link to PSOjbect. This function returns a PSObject with all scheduled task properties.")

## NOTES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-SchedulerTask\#notes "Direct link to NOTES")

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate"
title: "Get-UniversalDate · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Returns the date/time for the local culture in a universal sortable date time pattern.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UniversalDate [[-DateTime] <String>] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Converts the current datetime or a datetime string for the current culture into a universal sortable date time pattern, e.g.
2013-08-22 11:51:52Z

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UniversalDate

```

Returns the current date in a universal sortable date time pattern.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UniversalDate -DateTime '25/08/2013'

```

Returns the date for the current culture in a universal sortable date time pattern.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -DateTime [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#-datetime "Direct link to -DateTime")

Specify the DateTime in the current culture.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: ((Get-Date -Format ($culture).DateTimeFormat.UniversalDateTimePattern).ToString())
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UniversalDate\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

Continue if an error is encountered.
Default: $false.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Boolean
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: False
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-UserProfiles.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles"
title: "Get-UserProfiles · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Get the User Profile Path, User Account Sid, and the User Account Name for all users that log onto the machine and also the Default User (which does not log on).

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UserProfiles [[-ExcludeNTAccount] <String[]>] [[-ExcludeSystemProfiles] <Boolean>]
 [[-ExcludeServiceProfiles] <Boolean>] [-ExcludeDefaultUser] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Get the User Profile Path, User Account Sid, and the User Account Name for all users that log onto the machine and also the Default User (which does not log on).

Please note that the NTAccount property may be empty for some user profiles but the SID and ProfilePath properties will always be populated.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UserProfiles

```

Returns the following properties for each user profile on the system: NTAccount, SID, ProfilePath

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-UserProfiles -ExcludeNTAccount 'CONTOSO\Robot','CONTOSO\ntadmin'

```

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
[String[]]$ProfilePaths = Get-UserProfiles | Select-Object -ExpandProperty 'ProfilePath'

```

Returns the user profile path for each user on the system.
This information can then be used to make modifications under the user profile on the filesystem.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -ExcludeNTAccount [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#-excludentaccount "Direct link to -ExcludeNTAccount")

Specify NT account names in Domain\\Username format to exclude from the list of user profiles.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String[]
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ExcludeSystemProfiles [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#-excludesystemprofiles "Direct link to -ExcludeSystemProfiles")

Exclude system profiles: SYSTEM, LOCAL SERVICE, NETWORK SERVICE.
Default is: $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Boolean
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: True
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ExcludeServiceProfiles [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#-excludeserviceprofiles "Direct link to -ExcludeServiceProfiles")

Exclude service profiles where NTAccount begins with NT SERVICE.
Default is: $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Boolean
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 3

```

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

### None [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#none "Direct link to None")

### You cannot pipe objects to this function. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#you-cannot-pipe-objects-to-this-function "Direct link to You cannot pipe objects to this function.")

## OUTPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-UserProfiles\#outputs "Direct link to OUTPUTS")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Get-WindowTitle.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle"
title: "Get-WindowTitle · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Search for an open window title and return details about the window.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

### SearchWinTitle [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#searchwintitle "Direct link to SearchWinTitle")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-WindowTitle -WindowTitle <String> [-DisableFunctionLogging] [<CommonParameters>]

```

### GetAllWinTitles [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#getallwintitles "Direct link to GetAllWinTitles")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-WindowTitle [-GetAllWindowTitles] [-DisableFunctionLogging] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Search for a window title.
If window title searched for returns more than one result, then details for each window will be displayed.

Returns the following properties for each window: WindowTitle, WindowHandle, ParentProcess, ParentProcessMainWindowHandle, ParentProcessId.

Function does not work in SYSTEM context unless launched with "psexec.exe -s -i" to run it as an interactive process under the SYSTEM account.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-WindowTitle -WindowTitle 'Microsoft Word'

```

Gets details for each window that has the words "Microsoft Word" in the title.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-WindowTitle -GetAllWindowTitles

```

Gets details for all windows with a title.

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Get-WindowTitle -GetAllWindowTitles | Where-Object { $_.ParentProcess -eq 'WINWORD' }

```

Get details for all windows belonging to Microsoft Word process with name "WINWORD".

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -WindowTitle [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Get-WindowTitle\#-windowtitle "Direct link to -WindowTitle")

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Install-SCCMSoftwareUpdates\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Scans for outstanding SCCM updates to be installed and installs the pending updates.

Only compatible with SCCM 2012 Client or higher.
This function can take several minutes to run.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Install-SCCMSoftwareUpdates\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers"
title: "Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Set current user registry settings for all current users and any new users in the future.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers [-RegistrySettings] <ScriptBlock> [[-UserProfiles] <PSObject[]>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Set HKCU registry settings for all current and future users by loading their NTUSER.dat registry hive file, and making the modifications.

This function will modify HKCU settings for all users even when executed under the SYSTEM account.

To ensure new users in the future get the registry edits, the Default User registry hive used to provision the registry for new users is modified.

This function can be used as an alternative to using ActiveSetup for registry settings.

The advantage of using this function over ActiveSetup is that a user does not have to log off and log back on before the changes take effect.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
[ScriptBlock]$HKCURegistrySettings = {
    Set-RegistryKey -Key 'HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Office\14.0\Common' -Name 'qmenable' -Value 0 -Type DWord -SID $UserProfile.SID
    Set-RegistryKey -Key 'HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Office\14.0\Common' -Name 'updatereliabilitydata' -Value 1 -Type DWord -SID $UserProfile.SID
}

Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers -RegistrySettings $HKCURegistrySettings

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -RegistrySettings [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#-registrysettings "Direct link to -RegistrySettings")

Script block which contains HKCU registry settings which should be modified for all users on the system.
Must specify the -SID parameter for all HKCU settings.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: ScriptBlock
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -UserProfiles [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#-userprofiles "Direct link to -UserProfiles")

Specify the user profiles to modify HKCU registry settings for.
Default is all user profiles except for system profiles.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: PSObject[]
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: (Get-UserProfiles)
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

### None [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers\#none "Direct link to None")

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod"
title: "Invoke-ObjectMethod · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Invoke method on any object.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

### Positional (Default) [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#positional-default "Direct link to Positional (Default)")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Invoke-ObjectMethod [-InputObject] <Object> [-MethodName] <String> [[-ArgumentList] <Object[]>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

### Named [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#named "Direct link to Named")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Invoke-ObjectMethod [-InputObject] <Object> [-MethodName] <String> [-Parameter] <Hashtable>
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Invoke method on any object with or without using named parameters.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
$ShellApp = New-Object -ComObject 'Shell.Application'

```

$null = Invoke-ObjectMethod -InputObject $ShellApp -MethodName 'MinimizeAll'

Minimizes all windows.

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
$ShellApp = New-Object -ComObject 'Shell.Application'

```

$null = Invoke-ObjectMethod -InputObject $ShellApp -MethodName 'Explore' -Parameter @{'vDir'='C:\\Windows'}

Opens the C:\\Windows folder in a Windows Explorer window.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -InputObject [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#-inputobject "Direct link to -InputObject")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 2
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ArgumentList [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-ObjectMethod\#-argumentlist "Direct link to -ArgumentList")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL"
title: "Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Register or unregister a DLL file.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL [-FilePath] <String> [[-DLLAction] <String>] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Register or unregister a DLL file using regsvr32.exe.
Function can be invoked using alias: 'Register-DLL' or 'Unregister-DLL'.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Register-DLL -FilePath "C:\Test\DcTLSFileToDMSComp.dll"

```

Register DLL file using the "Register-DLL" alias for this function

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
UnRegister-DLL -FilePath "C:\Test\DcTLSFileToDMSComp.dll"

```

Unregister DLL file using the "Unregister-DLL" alias for this function

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL -FilePath "C:\Test\DcTLSFileToDMSComp.dll" -DLLAction 'Register'

```

Register DLL file using the actual name of this function

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -FilePath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#-filepath "Direct link to -FilePath")

Path to the DLL file.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -DLLAction [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#-dllaction "Direct link to -DLLAction")

Specify whether to register or unregister the DLL.
Optional if function is invoked using 'Register-DLL' or 'Unregister-DLL' alias.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Invoke-RegisterOrUnregisterDLL\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

Default is: $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Boolean
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 3
Default value: True
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

PeerDistributionPointProvisioning, ComplianceIntervalEnforcement, SoftwareUpdatesAgentAssignmentEvaluation, UploadStateMessage, StateMessageManager,

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Folder\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Folder\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_New-MsiTransform.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform"
title: "New-MsiTransform · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Create a transform file for an MSI database.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-MsiTransform [-MsiPath] <String> [[-ApplyTransformPath] <String>] [[-NewTransformPath] <String>]
 [-TransformProperties] <Hashtable> [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Create a transform file for an MSI database and create/modify properties in the Properties table.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
[Hashtable]$TransformProperties = {
    'ALLUSERS' = '1'
    'AgreeToLicense' = 'Yes'
    'REBOOT' = 'ReallySuppress'
    'RebootYesNo' = 'No'
    'ROOTDRIVE' = 'C:'
}
New-MsiTransform -MsiPath 'C:\Temp\PSADTInstall.msi' -TransformProperties $TransformProperties

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -MsiPath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#-msipath "Direct link to -MsiPath")

Specify the path to an MSI file.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ApplyTransformPath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#-applytransformpath "Direct link to -ApplyTransformPath")

Specify the path to a transform which should be applied to the MSI database before any new properties are created or modified.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -NewTransformPath [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#-newtransformpath "Direct link to -NewTransformPath")

Specify the path where the new transform file with the desired properties will be created.
If a transform file of the same name already exists, it will be deleted before a new one is created.

Default is: a) If -ApplyTransformPath was specified but not -NewTransformPath, then <ApplyTransformPath>.new.mst
b) If only -MsiPath was specified, then <MsiPath>.mst

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 3
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -TransformProperties [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#-transformproperties "Direct link to -TransformProperties")

Hashtable which contains calls to Set-MsiProperty for configuring the desired properties which should be included in new transform file.

Example hashtable: \[Hashtable\]$TransformProperties = @{ 'ALLUSERS' = '1' }

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Hashtable
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 4
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ContinueOnError [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-MsiTransform\#-continueonerror "Direct link to -ContinueOnError")

Default is: $true.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M

Position: 5
Default value: True
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Creates a new .lnk or .url type shortcut

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-Shortcut [-Path] <String> -TargetPath <String> [-Arguments <String>] [-IconLocation <String>]
 [-IconIndex <Int32>] [-Description <String>] [-WorkingDirectory <String>] [-WindowStyle <String>]
 [-RunAsAdmin] [-Hotkey <String>] [-ContinueOnError <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Creates a new shortcut .lnk or .url file, with configurable options

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-Shortcut -Path "$envProgramData\Microsoft\Windows\Start Menu\My Shortcut.lnk" -TargetPath "$envWinDir\System32\notepad.exe" -IconLocation "$envWinDir\System32\notepad.exe" -Description 'Notepad' -WorkingDirectory "$envHomeDrive\$envHomePath"

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-Shortcut\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Create a new zip archive or add content to an existing archive.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

### CreateFromDirectory (Default) [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#createfromdirectory-default "Direct link to CreateFromDirectory (Default)")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-ZipFile [-DestinationArchiveDirectoryPath] <String> [-DestinationArchiveFileName] <String>
 [-SourceDirectoryPath] <String[]> [-RemoveSourceAfterArchiving] [-OverWriteArchive]
 [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

### CreateFromFile [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#createfromfile "Direct link to CreateFromFile")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-ZipFile [-DestinationArchiveDirectoryPath] <String> [-DestinationArchiveFileName] <String>
 [-SourceFilePath] <String[]> [-RemoveSourceAfterArchiving] [-OverWriteArchive] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>]
 [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Create a new zip archive or add content to an existing archive by using the Shell object .CopyHere method.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
New-ZipFile -DestinationArchiveDirectoryPath 'E:\Testing' -DestinationArchiveFileName 'TestingLogs.zip' -SourceDirectory 'E:\Testing\Logs'

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/New-ZipFile\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Remove-Folder.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder"
title: "Remove-Folder · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Remove folder and files if they exist.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-Folder [-Path] <String> [-DisableRecursion] [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Remove folder and all files with or without recursion in a given path.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-Folder -Path "$envWinDir\Downloaded Program Files"

```

Deletes all files and subfolders in the Windows\\Downloads Program Files folder

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-Folder\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-Folder -Path "$envTemp\MyAppCache" -DisableRecursion

```

Deletes all files in the Temp\\MyAppCache folder but does not delete any subfolders.
