## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Remove-InvalidFileNameChars.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars"
title: "Remove-InvalidFileNameChars · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Remove invalid characters from the supplied string.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-InvalidFileNameChars [-Name] <String> [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Remove invalid characters from the supplied string and returns a valid filename as a string.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-InvalidFileNameChars -Name "Filename/\1"

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -Name [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#-name "Direct link to -Name")

Text to remove invalid filename characters from.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: True (ByPropertyName, ByValue)
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### CommonParameters [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#commonparameters "Direct link to CommonParameters")

This cmdlet supports the common parameters: -Debug, -ErrorAction, -ErrorVariable, -InformationAction, -InformationVariable, -OutVariable, -OutBuffer, -PipelineVariable, -Verbose, -WarningAction, and -WarningVariable. For more information, see [about\_CommonParameters](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=113216).

## INPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#inputs "Direct link to INPUTS")

### System.String [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#systemstring "Direct link to System.String")

### A string containing invalid filename characters. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#a-string-containing-invalid-filename-characters "Direct link to A string containing invalid filename characters.")

## OUTPUTS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#outputs "Direct link to OUTPUTS")

### System.String [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#systemstring-1 "Direct link to System.String")

### Returns the input string with the invalid characters removed. [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#returns-the-input-string-with-the-invalid-characters-removed "Direct link to Returns the input string with the invalid characters removed.")

## NOTES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#notes "Direct link to NOTES")

This functions always returns a string however it can be empty if the name only contains invalid characters.
Do no use this command for an entire path as '' is not a valid filename character.

## RELATED LINKS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-InvalidFileNameChars\#related-links "Direct link to RELATED LINKS")

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Remove-MSIApplications.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications"
title: "Remove-MSIApplications · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Removes all MSI applications matching the specified application name.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications [-Name] <String> [-Exact] [-WildCard] [[-Parameters] <String>]
 [[-AddParameters] <String>] [[-FilterApplication] <Array>] [[-ExcludeFromUninstall] <Array>]
 [-IncludeUpdatesAndHotfixes] [[-LoggingOptions] <String>] [[-private:LogName] <String>] [-PassThru]
 [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Removes all MSI applications matching the specified application name.
Enumerates the registry for installed applications matching the specified application name and uninstalls that application using the product code, provided the uninstall string matches "msiexec".

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Adobe Flash'

```

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Adobe Flash"

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Adobe'

```

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Adobe"

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Java 8 Update' -FilterApplication @(

```

@('Is64BitApplication', $false, 'Exact'),
@('Publisher', 'Oracle Corporation', 'Exact')
)

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Java 8 Update" where the software is 32-bits and the publisher is "Oracle Corporation".

### EXAMPLE 4 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-4 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 4")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Java 8 Update' -FilterApplication @(, @('Publisher', 'Oracle Corporation', 'Exact')) -ExcludeFromUninstall @(, @('DisplayName', 'Java 8 Update 45', 'Contains'))

```

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Java 8 Update" and also have "Oracle Corporation" as the Publisher; however, it does not uninstall "Java 8 Update 45" of the software.
NOTE: If only specifying a single row in the two-dimensional arrays, the array must have the extra parentheses and leading comma as in this example.

### EXAMPLE 5 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-5 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 5")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Java 8 Update' -ExcludeFromUninstall @(, @('DisplayName', 'Java 8 Update 45', 'Contains'))

```

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Java 8 Update"; however, it does not uninstall "Java 8 Update 45" of the software.
NOTE: If only specifying a single row in the two-dimensional array, the array must have the extra parentheses and leading comma as in this example.

### EXAMPLE 6 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#example-6 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 6")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-MSIApplications -Name 'Java 8 Update' -ExcludeFromUninstall @(

```

@('Is64BitApplication', $true, 'Exact'),
@('DisplayName', 'Java 8 Update 45', 'Exact'),
@('DisplayName', 'Java 8 Update 4\*', 'WildCard'),
@('DisplayName', 'Java \\d Update \\d{3}', 'RegEx'),
@('DisplayName', 'Java 8 Update', 'Contains'))

Removes all versions of software that match the name "Java 8 Update"; however, it does not uninstall 64-bit versions of the software, Update 45 of the software, or any Update that starts with 4.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -Name [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-name "Direct link to -Name")

The name of the application to uninstall.
Performs a contains match on the application display name by default.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: True
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Exact [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-exact "Direct link to -Exact")

### -FilterApplication [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-filterapplication "Direct link to -FilterApplication")

Two-dimensional array that contains one or more (property, value, match-type) sets that should be used to filter the list of results returned by Get-InstalledApplication to only those that should be uninstalled.
Properties that can be filtered upon: ProductCode, DisplayName, DisplayVersion, UninstallString, InstallSource, InstallLocation, InstallDate, Publisher, Is64BitApplication

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Array
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 4
Default value: @(@())
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -ExcludeFromUninstall [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-excludefromuninstall "Direct link to -ExcludeFromUninstall")

Two-dimensional array that contains one or more (property, value, match-type) sets that should be excluded from uninstall if found.
Properties that can be excluded: ProductCode, DisplayName, DisplayVersion, UninstallString, InstallSource, InstallLocation, InstallDate, Publisher, Is64BitApplication

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Array
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 5
Default value: @(@())
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -IncludeUpdatesAndHotfixes [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-includeupdatesandhotfixes "Direct link to -IncludeUpdatesAndHotfixes")

### -LoggingOptions [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-loggingoptions "Direct link to -LoggingOptions")

### -private:LogName [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-MSIApplications\#-private "Direct link to -private")

Overrides the default log file name.
The default log file name is generated from the MSI file name.
If LogName does not end in .log, it will be automatically appended.
For uninstallations, by default the product code is resolved to the DisplayName and version of the application.

## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Remove-RegistryKey.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey"
title: "Remove-RegistryKey · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Deletes the specified registry key or value.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-RegistryKey [-Key] <String> [[-Name] <String>] [-Recurse] [[-SID] <String>]
 [[-ContinueOnError] <Boolean>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Deletes the specified registry key or value.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-RegistryKey -Key 'HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\RunOnce'

```

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-RegistryKey -Key 'HKLM:SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run' -Name 'RunAppInstall'

```

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Remove-RegistryKey -Key 'HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Example' -Name '(Default)'

```

### -SID [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Remove-RegistryKey\#-sid "Direct link to -SID")

The security identifier (SID) for a user.
Specifying this parameter will convert a HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER registry key to the HKEY\_USERS$SID format.

Specify this parameter from the Invoke-HKCURegistrySettingsForAllUsers function to read/edit HKCU registry settings for all users on the system.

title: "Resolve-Error · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Enumerate error record details.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Resolve-Error [[-ErrorRecord] <Array>] [[-Property] <String[]>] [-GetErrorRecord] [-GetErrorInvocation]
 [-GetErrorException] [-GetErrorInnerException] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Enumerate an error record, or a collection of error record, properties.
By default, the details for the last error will be enumerated.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Resolve-Error

```

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Resolve-Error -Property *

```

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Resolve-Error -Property InnerException

```

### EXAMPLE 4 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#example-4 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 4")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Resolve-Error -GetErrorInvocation:$false

```

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -ErrorRecord [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#-errorrecord "Direct link to -ErrorRecord")

The error record to resolve.
The default error record is the latest one: $global:Error(0).
This parameter will also accept an array of error records.

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: Array
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: True (ByPropertyName, ByValue)
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

### -Property [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Resolve-Error\#-property "Direct link to -Property")

The list of properties to display from the error record.
Use "\*" to display all properties.

Default list of error properties is: Message, FullyQualifiedErrorId, ScriptStackTrace, PositionMessage, InnerException

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Type: String[]
Parameter Sets: (All)
Aliases:

Required: False
Position: 2
Default value: ('Message', 'InnerException', 'FullyQualifiedErrorId', 'ScriptStackTrace', 'PositionMessage')
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```


## File: psappdeploytoolkit.com_docs_3.10.2_reference_functions_Send-Keys.md

---
url: "https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys"
title: "Send-Keys · PSAppDeployToolkit"
---

[Skip to main content](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys#__docusaurus_skipToContent_fallback)

This is documentation for PSAppDeployToolkit **3.10.2 (Deprecated)**, which is no longer actively maintained.

For up-to-date documentation, see the **[latest version](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/introduction)** (4.1.0).

Version: 3.10.2 (Deprecated)

On this page

## SYNOPSIS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#synopsis "Direct link to SYNOPSIS")

Send a sequence of keys to one or more application windows.

## SYNTAX [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#syntax "Direct link to SYNTAX")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Send-Keys [[-WindowTitle] <String>] [-GetAllWindowTitles] [[-WindowHandle] <IntPtr>] [[-Keys] <String>]
 [[-WaitSeconds] <Int32>] [<CommonParameters>]

```

## DESCRIPTION [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#description "Direct link to DESCRIPTION")

Send a sequence of keys to one or more application window.
If window title searched for returns more than one window, then all of them will receive the sent keys.

Function does not work in SYSTEM context unless launched with "psexec.exe -s -i" to run it as an interactive process under the SYSTEM account.

## EXAMPLES [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#examples "Direct link to EXAMPLES")

### EXAMPLE 1 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#example-1 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 1")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Send-Keys -WindowTitle 'foobar - Notepad' -Key 'Hello world'

```

Send the sequence of keys "Hello world" to the application titled "foobar - Notepad".

### EXAMPLE 2 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#example-2 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 2")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Send-Keys -WindowTitle 'foobar - Notepad' -Key 'Hello world' -WaitSeconds 5

```

Send the sequence of keys "Hello world" to the application titled "foobar - Notepad" and wait 5 seconds.

### EXAMPLE 3 [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#example-3 "Direct link to EXAMPLE 3")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Send-Keys -WindowHandle ([IntPtr]17368294) -Key 'Hello world'

```

Send the sequence of keys "Hello world" to the application with a Window Handle of '17368294'.

## PARAMETERS [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#parameters "Direct link to PARAMETERS")

### -WindowTitle [​](https://psappdeploytoolkit.com/docs/3.10.2/reference/functions/Send-Keys\#-windowtitle "Direct link to -WindowTitle")

```codeBlockLines_Fl5M
Parameter Sets: (All)

Required: False
Position: 1
Default value: None
Accept pipeline input: False
Accept wildcard characters: False

```

